Your timetable depends on the core courses andelectives you take. How long is the internship and when can we start? Internships last 4 to 6 months and they usually take place after the final term has ended.Students start sourcing for internships as early as while they are in the program. Our CareerServices Team is there to guide you with your internship sourcing. How does ESSEC help me upon arrival? Once you have confirmed your seat in the program, the Office of the Registrar will provideyou with the necessary information to complete your administrative enrolment. All new students undergo an induction, which includes an overview of the program structure andcurriculum, academic and administrative guidelines, student life and career services. What student clubs exist in ESSEC? What if I want to start a new club? There are numerous cultural, professional, community and athletic clubs at ESSEC APAC. How can I find accommodation in Singapore? Does ESSEC Asia-Pacific offer accommodation? The School does not offer accommodation but fret not as finding accommodation in Singapore is easy. The School provides support in your search for the ideal housing option that meets your needs and budget. Please visit our blogsite for more info. “ESSEC Career Services team is extremely supportive and helps in the journey of finding the right internship”Yue NingMSc MMD’21 ESSEC Career ServicesThroughout your time at ESSEC, the Career Services will accompany you in defining your career plan and facilitating your entry into the professional world. Career guidance and advice Throughout your time at ESSEC Business School, the Career Services will accompany you in defining your career plan and facilitating your entry into the professional world. Through the support of the Career Services team, you will be able to: Learn more about yourself and enhance your experiences. Explore career opportunities, reflect and develop your personal and professional project. Define your internship/job search strategy and prepare yourself for numerous recruitment events through coaching with specialists Prepare your CV, LinkedIn profile and cover letter in an impactful manner, and develop your network efficiently. Prepare for different types of job interviews through role-playing exercises (pitching) and learn to position yourself well during salary negotiations. Each year, there are: 17 000 exclusive job postings : internships, apprenticeships and jobs. 430+ meetings with recruiters based in France and all around the world : job fairs, company presentations and case studies. 4 000+ individual appointments with career consultants. Access to 5 learning platforms and 40+ articles, training and self-teaching modules 164 career related workshops Meeting with professionals and recruitment opportunities The Career Services team organizes numerous recruitment events and puts you in direct contact with your future employer(s): - Networking, professional meetings - Company presentations, business conferences, recruitment sessions, workshops, master classes and internationally-themed weeks. Recruitment Fairs Organized at ESSECTalent Days This recruitment fair brings companies to our students. You will establish contacts with companies from all sectors of activity, such as: LVMH, Capgemini Invent, Sodexo, DBS, Standard Chartered Bank, etc. ESSEC Alumni: A network For Life When you join ESSEC Business School, you join a community and will discover the power of the ESSEC network. ESSEC Alumni already has 71,000 graduates with diverse profiles dispersed in all corners of the world. With unique personalities, they share a common goal: to achieve their career objectives. As you enter ESSEC, you become a member of ESSEC Alumni and you remain one forever. This is the lifetime membership, that ESSEC has been the first French Business School with a global reach to put in place. ESSEC Alumni is by your side at every stage of your career: When you are a student, to guide you in finding professional opportunities through the network, exchanging with graduates, benefiting from various services to launch your start-up, and staying up to date with the latest news from the ESSEC community. When you are a graduate, to support you throughout your professional life, help you develop your network and exchange with your peers, guide you in benefiting from services for your start-up, and allow you to rediscover the atmosphere of your ESSEC years. Entrepreneurship & InnovationSince its creation, ESSEC has always cultivated a spirit of entrepreneurship and innovation, which lies at the very core of its educational approach, research, and managerial practices. ESSEC Ventures is a structure that supports ESSEC students with business projects. It consists of an incubator, a talent incubator, and a seed fund. It also organizes numerous events bringing together entrepreneurs and investors. ESSEC Antropia is a structure that supports ESSEC students with social enterprise projects so that social, environmental, and economic considerations can come together to create a better world. Can I get a Long Term Visit Pass (LTVP) in Singapore at the end of the program? Yes, subject to having already obtained a Students Pass in Singapore, which comes with a FIN number that is used to apply for the Long Term Visit Pass (LTVP) in Singapore. The student must also be in Singapore with a valid pass (Students Pass or Visit Pass with at least 10 days remaining) when they submit the application. The LTVP allows foreign students to remain in Singapore for one year after finishing their studies in Singapore to look for employment opportunities (This applies even if the student has done only a trimester at the end of his/her program in Singapore). For more information regarding the application process, please visit this page. How and where do I find internships in Asia? The Career Services in Singapore is very active and well connected. They organise many events and tend to have a smaller more responsive network of partner companies. ESSEC is well known in the region and has a good reputation with the companies who know and work with us. The school is constantly working to establish more partnerships and networks. Past students have worked in a huge variety of sectors and tend to be based in Singapore, Hong Kong, Tokyo, Dubai, etc. As an intern, salaries are low but as a graduate, starting salaries are relatively high and you progress very quickly, more so than maybe in Europe. Have you obtained or are currently pursuing a Master/4-year bachelor/3-year bachelor’s degree in any field of study (engineering, science, mathematics, business, law, humanities & social sciences, economics, etc.)? Are you a high-potential candidate looking to gain or deepen your knowledge of Marketing? Are you open-minded, internationally oriented and have leadership potential? STEP 1: Anticipate, prepare and take the testsYou will need to provide: - 1 English test score - mandatory. Exempted if the candidate has completed at least 3 years in a higher education program in English at a 100% English-speaking institution. In that case, please provide us an official certificate with the mention that the medium of instruction is English. Test Validity TOEFL iBT, TOEFL iBT Special at Home Edition The English tests must not be older than 2 years at the application deadline (application round you choose to apply in) Minimum score 95 Institution Code: 0520 Special home edition is accepted IELTS (Academic) Minimum score 6.5 Cambridge (Minimum FCE) Minimum score 175 TOEIC (Listening and Reading) Minimum score 850 It can take several months to prepare and register for an exam slot for these tests. Keep this in mind before starting your application as without these test scores uploaded in your application file, it will be incomplete. The management test (TAGE MAGE , GMAT or GRE) is optional but can add value to your application. STEP 2: Start your online applicationPlease fill in an online application. Create your account and you will receive an email with your login and pin number. These are required each time you sign in, so keep them safe! You can fill in the application form at our own pace and come back to it at any point. STEP 3: Upload your supporting documentsA complete application file includes the following items. Incomplete applications will not be processed. All documents must be provided in English, including the Application Form. Official translations must be provided for documents in other languages by a certified translator. Items Description Curriculum Vitae 1 page maximum - in English Degree(s) obtained Authenticated copies of accredited degrees since high school (school leaving). While applying, if you do not have your final diploma that makes you eligible for the program, you can apply with an Enrolment Certificate, with an expected graduation date. Important: By mid-December of your starting year at ESSEC, you will have to provide a copy of your diploma (or a certificate of completion). Transcripts/Grade Sheets Official or authenticated transcript copies of all academic terms attended since high school, including exchange programs (simple copies will not be accepted). Grading Scale details must be provided. 2 x References One academic and one professional reference is highly recommended. It is the applicants responsibility to enter details of both the referees as soon as possible to allow them to send the online recommendation on time. Once you enter their details and save, a link is sent to them immediately to fill out the recommendation online. 1 English Test Copy of official score (test taker version) 1 Identity Card Passport or National Identity Card. 1 Photograph A recent ID photo Application Fee 115 € non-refundable and payable only online Click here to see if you are exempted STEP 4: Submit your applicationOnce you have completed your online application and have attached all the supporting documents, the final step is to submit your online application. Once you have submitted your application online, you cannot make changes to your application. Please keep in mind that there are several rounds of admissions. The deadlines to submit your application are listed in the table at the top of this page. STEP 5: Sit your interview Shortlisted applicants may be contacted for an interview via videoconference. The objective of the interview is: - To understand you better: your personality and your values- To evaluate your professional and personal project and its coherence with the program STEP 6: Get your admission results Your application will be assessed by the Academic Directors and an admissions committee. You will be notified about the results by email (refer to the above mentioned timetable). If you have been successful, you will then be contacted by the Admissions Office to inform you how to confirm your place in the program. STEP 7: Secure your seatFollowing your admission, make sure to secure your seat in the program by paying the non-refundable deposit within 2 weeks. This amount will be deducted from your tuition fee. Welcome to ESSEC! Is prior professional experience required? Although prior professional experience is not a mandatory requirement, having some relevant work experience does help you with your application to get into the program. How important are the references?References are very important. The admissions committee is used to looking at these and the ones that make the difference outline concrete examples of how the student lives up to the praise/recommendations given. You should therefore select references who know you best and have experience of working with you either academically or professionally. It is much better to have a reference from someone who knows you than from someone you have selected due to their position. Is a certain level of French required for the MMD program?While students have the chance to learn French during the program, MMD does not require any French proficiency as it is taught entirely in English. English is also the lingua franca in Singapore. Valid for 2025 Intake EU citizens NON-EU Citizens Total Tuition SGD 42,000 SGD 47,000 Administrative fee The non-refundable administrative fee is payable within two weeks from the day of admission and is deducted from the total tuition fee SGD 7,200 SGD 7,200 Remaining Tuition Fee The remaining tuition fee is payable before August 31st of the academic year SGD 34,800 SGD 39,800 Service Fee The service fee is payable once in addition to the total tuition fee before joining ESSEC (irrespective of the duration of the program) SGD 3,160 SGD 3,300 Scholarships ESSEC Academic Excellence ScholarshipsDescription: To sustain the academic excellence of the program, ESSEC Business School offers scholarships to the most outstanding candidates. Eligibility: Open to all applicants and awarded on the basis of the overall quality of their application i.e. academic excellence demonstrated in the file and during the interview. Amount: Up to 35% of total tuition fees. Procedure: Scholarship decisions are made during the application procedure. There is no additional application to fill out or request to make. Selected students will be notified upon being offered a place on the program. ESSEC Diversity ScholarshipDescription: Varied cultural perspectives and backgrounds enhance the education and experience of all our students as well as being a key factor in the excellence of our programs. With this in mind, ESSEC seeks to create further diversity in its already diverse student body. Eligibility: Open to applicants who are citizens of a country in one of the following regions: Asia-Pacific (excluding Singapore), Africa, Europe, North America and South America. Amount: Up to 30% of total tuition fees. Procedure: Scholarship decisions are made during the application procedure. They are awarded to applicants having demonstrated academic excellence and a strong international background in both their application file. Selected students will be notified upon being offered a place on the program. ESSEC Singapore Leaders ScholarshipDescription: This prestigious scholarship is awarded to outstanding candidates admitted to ESSECs Masters programs at the Asia-Pacific campus in Singapore. Open to Singaporean citizens and Permanent Residents, the scholarship aims to empower top talent with the education and skills needed to excel on the global stage. Eligibility: Candidates must be Singaporean citizens or Permanent Residents of Singapore. Amount: The scholarship will cover up to 50% of the total tuition fees. Procedure: This scholarship is awarded during each admission session alongside the admission offer. No additional application or request is required. Selected students will be notified upon receiving their admission offer. Lee Kuan Yew Scholarship DESCRIPTION: The Lee Kuan Yew (LKY) Scholarship is the premier postgraduate scholarship in Singapore. Set up in 1991, the scholarship marks Singapores continuous effort to recognize outstanding individuals with the aptitude and inclination to contribute to Singapore and its society. ELIGIBILITY: Candidates holding Singaporean citizenship will undergo a comprehensive evaluation on their leadership potential and accomplishments in their respective fields. Candidates should also demonstrate the potential to thrive in their professions, ultimately contributing to Singapore and its advancement. AMOUNT: Scholarship recipients will receive full tuition fees coverage and an annual allowance of S$50,000 for up to 2 years if they are pursuing a Master’s degree. PROCEDURE: Candidates can apply via the Public Service Commission Portal (Singpass login required). All applications will need to be supported by referee reports and submitted online by 28 February 2025. Student Loans FranceAs an ESSEC student, you can take out a preferential-rate bank loan, which covers full tuition and is repaid starting at the end of your first year of work. ESSEC has developed a partnership with major French bank branches located in Cergy (LCL, BNP Paribas and Société Générale) to give you special terms and conditions. Loan applicants are required to have a guarantor living in France. According to the banks, the guarantor must earn enough to cover the monthly loan payments but also be a French citizen, a close family member and/or both. Additional fees and expenses will be the responsibility of the student. Prodigy FinanceInternational Students from 150 different nationalities admitted to the MSc in Marketing Management and Digital may now apply to Prodigy Finance loans. Contrary to the banks in France, Prodigy does not require a collateral or co-signer. These loans are granted on the students future earning potential and don’t take into account credit history. Students may apply online on the Prodigy website. There is no hidden fee or early repayment fee. Interest rates may vary depending on individual profiles. Funds are directly disbursed to the school in euro (€) so no exchange rates are borne by the student. Disbursement starts from September and loan application processing time may go up to a month and a half. The sooner you apply, the better. We advise you to check your eligibility on the Prodigy website before applying. US Federal & Private LoansMany US citizens or permanent residents opt to take out the US Federal Stafford and private Sallie Mae loans. These loans can cover up to the full cost of attendance and all applicants having a co-signer in the US are eligible for these loan programmes. ESSEC is listed as “ESSEC Business School", and has a code number of G30959. The program has a strong international dimension and teaches students to adapt to a multicultural environment, addressing multinational issues and providing exposure to both Europe and Asia. It offers a global approach to finance with a strong emphasis on the underlying skills necessary to operate in today’s financial professions. 80% Hold degrees in Economics, Business and Finance 20% Hold degrees in Engineering and Sciences 23 Average age 30% Women Recognized by the French Ministry of Higher Education, Research and InnovationThe ESSEC Master in Finance program is authorized by the French Ministry of Higher Education, Research and Innovation to award a recognised BAC+5 degree, Master’s Grade, to its students. Authorisation is delivered following assessment by the National Management Programmes Assessment Commission (Commission d’Evaluation des Formations de Gestion - https://www.cefdg.fr) for a renewable period. This Commission undertakes assessment for all programs, with or without the Master’s Grade, delivered by business schools that are recognised by the French State to guarantee the quality of teaching delivered and the value of their degree. This is valid whether you do your program at France campus or at Singapore campus. CFA InstituteCFA Institute - Qualify as an international Chartered Financial Analyst If you are looking to make a career as a consultant in mergers and acquisitions, project financing, as an equity analyst, fixed income analyst, portfolio manager, equity salesperson, etc., you can prepare while studying at ESSEC by passing the CFA Institute exam to become a “Chartered Financial Analyst” which is the internationally recognized qualification. Furthermore, every year, Master in Finance students represent ESSEC to the CFA Institute Research Challenge. In Feb 2019, ESSEC won the French final and qualified for the EMEA final. “Welcome to France”- Campus France ESSEC Business School has been recognized by Campus France and the Ministry of Higher Education and Research for the quality of its international students’ welcome. The school received the highest level that can be obtained from the "Bienvenue en France" certification, which is the third level. This certification recognizes the quality of ESSECs reception in all the criteria provided: The quality and accessibility of information The welcoming of new international students The academic offer Accommodations Campus life The quality of post-graduate follow-up Triple Crown AccreditationThe academic excellence of ESSEC’s programs is recognized through its international standards in management training, and it holds the prestigious “Triple Crown of accreditations: EQUIS, AACSB, and AMBA. Academic experience The duration of the Master in Finance is 2 years (Master 1+Master 2) or 1 year (Master 2 only), depending on your latest degree. Professional experience Each year (M1 & M2), students will complete an internship with a duration of 4 to 6 months; it can take place anywhere in the world and is designed to facilitate students’ professional integration. The academic dissertation is an alternative option to the internship (during M2). It represents independent and individual research on cutting-edge topics related to any field of finance. International experience Students get a chance to participate in 2 Study Trips to London and Hong Kong or New York. The MIF program has a strong analytical focus and aims to provide you with a comprehensive view of finance enabling you to develop and become a fully-operational professional. According to your professional project, you may choose to apply in the program either on the ESSEC France campus (Cergy, Paris area), or the ESSEC Asia-Pacific campus (Singapore). Master 1 in France or Singapore Depending on your latest degree, you will start the program in M1 and the total duration of the program is 2 years (M1+M2). To build up your strength and help you build your foundations, you will begin the program with a term (T0) of preparatory courses in Finance, Mathematics and Statistics. Examples of courses include: Financial Theory Statistics Foundations of Calculus & Probability During the following term (T1), you will follow 6 courses from a general track (1 compulsory & 5 electives). Through this first year, you will be able to discover your professional interest, to help you decide on which track to choose in Year 2 (M2). Example of courses include: Programming in Python Management Control Strategic Cost Management Sustainability Performance Macroeconomic Theory and Development See the full list of courses. You will do a 6-month internship at the end of M1. Master 2 in France or SingaporeDepending on your latest degree, you will start the program in M2 and the total duration of the program is 1 year (M2), or you will continue with the second year of the program (M2) if you started in M1. This year (M2) is divided into three terms, where you will cover: courses, 2 study trips to the major financial centers (London and New York or Hong Kong), specialized tracks, certificates in FinTech & Analytics, Energy & Commodities, andor/ AMF certification (optional), and an internship or academic dissertation. Terms 0 & 1. Build your Foundations In France (Paris area) or in Singapore, during these first terms you will take core courses and electives. Examples of courses include: Corporate Financial Management Financial Markets Options Programming in Python Big Data Analytics International Finance Terms 2 & 3. Choose your Track To tailor the program to your career goals, you will follow core and elective courses on the specialization of your choice: Corporate Finance Track, Financial Markets Track, Fintech & Analytics Track. Examples or courses include: Examples or courses include France or Singapore Corporate Finance France or Singapore Financial Markets SingaporeFintech & Analytics Core courses Mergers and Acquisitions Firm Valuation Private Equity Fixed Income Advanced Derivative Markets Volatility Trading Digital Financial Platforms & Intermediation Financial Econometrics Big Data Analytics Elective courses Wealth Management Portfolio Theory & Investment Analysis Coaching CFA Commodity Markets & Energy Products Financial Risk Management Advanced Derivative Market Financial Econometrics Energy & Commodity Markets & Products Digital Financial Platforms and Intermediation See the full list of courses. During term 2 you will also have the possibility to do inter-campus mobility. International Study TripsDuring M2, ESSEC Master in Finance offers a unique opportunity for students to travel to two of the major financial hubs (London and Hong Kong or New York). The study trips allow privileged access to the most prestigious investment banks and consulting firms such as: Barclays Capital, Bank of America-Merrill Lynch, BNP-Paribas, Crédit Suisse, Goldman Sachs, J.P. Morgan, etc. Students not only meet and exchange views with professionals but also get to interact with ESSEC alumni. Deepen Your Knowledge with Certificates During the M2 you will have opportunities to get a certificate in Energy and Commodities. The Energy and Commodity Finance Research Center at ESSEC Business School aims at promoting research and disseminating knowledge in the field of commodity markets and energy finance. This goal is pursued by undertaking research projects and hosting activities for incentivizing interaction across disciplines including finance, economics, financial mathematics, operations research, and management science. Focus is put on bridging international collaborations among researchers at a worldwide level. The center organizes scientific conferences, runs a monthly webinar, supervises a dedicated graduate track, and manages Argo Review, a journal devoted to cutting-edge knowledge in the field. The Master in Finance is built on the premise of learning by doing. Each year, students (M1 & M2) complete an internship with a duration of 4 to 6 months; it can take place anywhere in the world and is designed to let you integrate into the professional world. Students are also enrolled in summer and graduate programs during the Master in Finance program. ESSEC is in partnership with AlumnEye, a network designed to help students to prepare for interviews in Investment Banking, Market Finance and Strategy Consulting. It trains students for the selection process of the most prestigious financial institutions. This interactive and personalized training, taking place at the beginning of the academic year. It allows students to stand out from the thousands of applications, and facilitates significant access to summer internships and graduate programs. In that case, please provide us an official certificate with the mention that the medium of instruction is English. TEST VALIDITY* Management Test GMAT Exam, GMAT, GMAT Online, or GMAT Focus Edition 5 years Select "ESSEC Business School-Master in Finance" GRE or GRE Test at Home (Verbal Reasoning, Quantitative Reasoning and Analytical Writing) 5 years Institution Code: 0839 Tage-Mage 2 years CAT 1 year For Indian applicants English Test TOEFL iBT, TOEFL iBT Special at Home Edition The English tests must not be older than 2 years at the application deadline (application round you choose to apply in) Minimum score 95 Institution Code: 0520 IELTS Academic Minimum score 6.5 Cambridge B2 First Minimum Minimum score 175 TOEIC Listening and Reading Minimum score 850 It can take several months to prepare and register for an exam slot for these tests. Keep this in mind before starting your application as without these test scores uploaded in your application file, it will be incomplete. Click here to take the GMAT Quiz and get an estimate of your score. Please note that you cannot apply with a GMAT Quiz score. STEP 2: Start your online applicationCreate your candidate account. You can fill in the online application at your own pace and come back to it at any point. You can only apply once per program each academic year. Once validated, your campus choice is final. STEP 3: Upload your supporting documentsA complete application file includes the following items. Incomplete application will not be processed. All documents must be provided in English or French (except the CV). Official translations must be provided for documents in other languages by a certified translator. Items Description Curriculum Vitae 1 page maximum - in English Motivation Letter 1 page maximum - in English Degree(s) obtained Authenticated copies of accredited degrees since high school (school leaving). While applying, if you do not have your final diploma that makes you eligible for the program, you can apply with an Enrolment Certificate, with an expected graduation date. Important: By mid-December of your starting year at ESSEC, you will have to provide a copy of your diploma (or a certificate of completion). Transcripts/Grade Sheets Authenticated copies of official transcripts, by chronological order, for all academic terms attended since high school, including exchange programs, repeated years, preparatory classes, grading system details and double degree (simple copies and screenshots are not accepted). If your studies have been interrupted, please add a letter with the academic year concerned and explain the reasons (gap year, illness, change of direction, travel, employment, leave, internship, etc.).Grading Scale details must also be provided. 2 x References One academic and one professional reference is highly recommended. It is the applicants responsibility to enter details of both the referees as soon as possible to allow them to send the online recommendation on time. Once you enter their details and save, a link is sent to them immediately to fill out the recommendation online. 1 Management Test Copy of official score (test taker version) 1 English Test 1 Certificate for Athletes (if applicable) A certificate for High Level Athlete (HLA) or Certificate of Aptitude for Sports Practice is required. The certificate must be valid at the time of application. 1 Identity Card Passport or National Identity Card (only for EU citizens) 1 Photograph A recent ID photo Application Fee €100 non-refundable and payable online onlyClick to see if you are exempted STEP 4: Submit your applicationOnce you have completed your online application and have attached all the supporting documents, the final step is to submit your online application. Once you have submitted your application online, you cannot make changes to your application. Please keep in mind that there are several rounds of admissions. The deadlines to submit your application are listed in the table above. STEP 5: Get your resultsYour application will be assessed by the Academic Directors and an admissions committee. You will be notified about the results by email (refer to the above mentioned calendar). If you have been successful, you will then be contacted by the Admissions Office to inform you how to confirm your place in the program. If you applied for one-year program, please note that if the commission board finds that your experience or background is strong but not complete enough in some required aspects, you may be asked to join the two-year program instead in order to build up your strength and ensure your success. STEP 6: Secure your seatFollowing your admission, make sure to secure your seat in the program by paying the non-refundable deposit within 2 weeks. This amount will be deducted from your tuition fee. Do you need more information?You need more information to prepare your application? Please refer to this link for insights on our application portal. How important are the references?References are very important. The admissions committee is used to looking at these and the ones that make the difference outline concrete examples of how the student lives up to the praise/recommendations given. You should therefore select references who know you best and have experience of working with you either academically or professionally. It is much better to have a reference from someone who knows you than from someone you have selected due to their position. How important is the GMAT score?The GMAT is a very important part of your application. It is mandatory and we encourage you to get ready for the GMAT exam in advance. You should aim for as high a GMAT score as you can possibly achieve. Is a certain level of French required for the program?No, the program is taught in English and all of the staff members speak English. You have the chance to learn French during your program.However, we strongly recommend you try and learn French when you are here. Acquiring the language does help you during your time at ESSEC and in France. If you want to remain in France for your internship or job in the future, learning French is fundamental. How will my application be evaluated?Every application is thoroughly reviewed by the admissions board which is composed of both academic and professional staff, with consideration given to all elements including hard and soft skills. Prodigy FinanceInternational Students from 150 different nationalities admitted to the MSc in Marketing Management and Digital may now apply to Prodigy Finance loans. Students may apply online on the Prodigy website. There is no hidden fee or early repayment fee. Interest rates may vary depending on individual profiles. This intensive, full-time program offers a comprehensive view of data sciences and business analytics, combining theoretical foundations with practical applications. 58% Hold degrees in Economics, Business and Finance 35% Hold degrees in Engineering and Sciences 7% Hold degrees in Languages and Social Sciences 23 Average age 39% Women 78% International students "If I had to describe the program in three words, I would say its challenging, motivational and rewarding".Mathieu KREMETH DSBA21 Recognized by the French Ministry of Higher Education, Research and InnovationThe ESSEC/ CentraleSupélec Master in Data Sciences and Business Analytics program is authorized by the French Ministry of Higher Education, Research and Innovation to award a recognised BAC+5 degree, Master’s Grade, to its students. Authorisation is delivered following assessment by the National Management Programmes Assessment Commission (Commission d’Evaluation des Formations de Gestion - https://www.cefdg.fr) for a renewable period. This Commission undertakes assessment for all programs, with or without the Master’s Grade, delivered by business schools that are recognised by the French State to guarantee the quality of teaching delivered and the value of their degree. This is valid whether you do your program at France campus or at Singapore campus. “Welcome to France”- Campus FranceESSEC Business School has been recognized by Campus France and the Ministry of Higher Education, Research and Innovation for the quality of its international students’ welcome. The school received the highest level that can be obtained from the "Bienvenue en France" certification, which is the third level. This certification recognizes the quality of ESSECs reception in all the criteria provided: The quality and accessibility of information The welcoming of new international students The academic offer Accommodations Campus life The quality of post-graduate follow-up Triple Crown Accreditation The academic excellence of ESSEC’s programs is recognized through its international standards in management training, and it holds the prestigious ”Triple Crown of accreditations: EQUIS, AACSB, and AMBA. For a global understanding of the challenges underlying the digital era and to master the science of data and the techniques of business analytics, the program has a strong scientific focus and aims to provide students with a comprehensive view of these complementary and intrinsically linked fields, enabling them to develop as fully-operational professionals. Academic Experience: Possibility to choose one out of seven specilaizations: Finance, Healthcare, Marketing, Retail, Consulting, Research & International.Besides the classes the studnets will have a chance to participate in the annual Hackaton, the Corporate reaserach Project and in various Masterclasses International Experience: Students get a chance to participate in an International Field Trip in Europe Professional Experience: Kickstart your career with a minimum 4-month internship at leading companies in the data sector Master 2 (M2)Paris campusA year to master the science of data and the techniques of business analytics, and tailor the program to your specific career goals Term 1 Core Courses Machine Learning, Optimization, Forecasting, Deep learning, etc... Term 2 Data science elective courses from your chosen sector : Finance, Healthcare, Marketing, Retail, Consulting, & Research Term 3 Business analytics elective courses from your chosen sector or International studies at ESSEC Singapore campus Summer Minimum 4 months compulsory internship or professional experience Master 1 If you start the program in M1, the total duration of the program will be 2 years (M1+M2). To build up your strength and help you build your foundations, you will begin the program with a first term of foundations in mathematics Refresher courses and foundation of data science. During the second and third term you will follow management and business core courses, as well as foundation of business analytics. You will also participate in the hackathon organized by Ekimetrics and Artefact. Through this first year, you will be able to discover your professional interest, to help you decide on which specialization to choose in Year 2 (M2). Examples of core courses include: Probability & Statistics Linear Algebra Algorithm, Python, C++ Optimization Econometrics 1 Introduction to Machine Learning Finance Game Theory Strategy & Management Data-driven Marketing Decision Theory Business Economics You can do a 4 month internship at the end of M1. Master 2This year (M2) is divided into three terms where you will master the science of data, the techniques of business analytics and specialize in one the seven specializations. Courses are tailor to your specific career goals while being highly specialized in content and addressing recent trends and challenges. At the end of term 1 you will choose your specialization from Finance, Healthcare, Marketing, Retail, Consulting, Research & International. Term 1: Build your Foundations During the tem 1 you will follow the core courses like Machine Learning 1 and 2 Deep learning 1 and 2 Cyber Securuty Machine Learning in Network Science Economectrics 2 etc. Term 2 & 3: Elective courses from your chosen specialization During the terms 2 & 3 you will follow the data science and business analytics elective courses from your chosen specialization. Specializations At the end of term 1 you will choose one of the 7 specializations offered by the program. 1. Finance In the finance specialization students will learn how to leverage AI and data analytics to optimize financial strategies, manage risks, and predict market trends. They will develop skills in financial modeling, algorithmic trading, and fraud detection. Core courses include: Financial Econometrics, Financial Markets Trading, Digital Transformations of Markets, and Fintech etc. Professional Paths: Financial Analyst Quantitative Analyst Risk Manager Portfolio Manager Financial Data Scientist 2. Healthtech The healthtech specialization focuses on the application of AI and data science in healthcare. Students will explore technologies that improve patient care, streamline hospital operations, and enhance medical research. Core courses include: Medical Imaging, Analytics in Healthcare, AI in Healthcare etc. Professional Paths: Health Data Analyst Bioinformatics Specialist Clinical Data Scientist Healthcare Consultant Medical AI Researcher 3. Marketing & Consumer In marketing and consumer, students will learn to use data-driven insights to shape marketing strategies, understand consumer behavior, and personalize customer experiences. Core courses include: Business Intelligence, Omnichannel Digital Strategies, Gen AI fundamentals, Impacts & Project development Professional Paths: Marketing Analyst Consumer Insights Specialist Digital Marketing Manager CRM Analyst Market Researcher 4. Retailtech, Supply & Sustainability This combined sector focuses on the application of AI and data science to optimize retail operations, supply chains, and promote sustainability. Students will learn to enhance the retail experience, streamline logistics, reduce waste, and improve supply network efficiency. Core courses include: Supply Chain Analytics, Machine Learning in Network Science, Data Vizualisation Professional Paths: Retail Data Scientist E-commerce Analyst Inventory Optimization Specialist Supply Chain Analyst Sustainability Consultant Operations Manager Retail Strategy Consultant 5. Consulting & Strategy Consulting and Strategy focus on using AI and data analytics to solve complex business problems and devise strategic initiatives. Students will develop expertise in data-driven decision-making and business transformation. Core courses include: Decision Analysis, Advanced Applications of AI in Business and Data Monetization, Blockchain Professional Paths: Business Analyst Strategy Consultant Management Consultant Data Strategy Manager Business Intelligence Analyst 6. Research The research specialization prepares students for careers in academic and industrial research, focusing on developing new AI and data science methodologies. Students will engage in cutting-edge research projects and contribute to the advancement of the field. Core courses include: Computer Vision, Natural Language Processing, Deep Learning in Practice Professional Paths: Research Scientist Data Science Researcher AI Research Engineer Academic Researcher R&D Specialist 7. International (Singapore) This specialization equips the students with a global business perspective, focusing on Asian economies and cybersecurity. Students will apply data science to regional business challanges, exploring the role of analytics in economic growth and digital security within Singapores dynamic economy. Core courses include: Asian Economies, Sequential Prediction, Optimization & Investment, Cyber Security Professional Paths: Global Data Analyst: Analyze business data in the context of Asian markets Cybersecurity Data Scientist: Mitigate cyber risks using data science Business Intelligence Consultant (Asia): Advise on data strategies for multinational businesses Global Supply Chain Analyst: Optimize supply chains in Asia using analytics Economic Data Strategist (Asia): Provide insights on regional economic trends Hands-on Field ExperienceThe Master in Data Sciences & Business Analytics is built on the premise of learning by doing. That is to say, we dont want you to just theorize about your chosen field of expertise, but to experience it and to delve into the complexity of business life in the real world. Hackathons Each year (M1 & M2), you will complete and validate a Hackathon - a project spread over a few days organized and monitored together with a partner company- requiring innovative ideas for analyzing and visualizing data. Some partner companies are Ekimetrics and Artefact. Corporate Research Project The Corporate Research Project spans January-June of M2. Students work in teams to solve key strategic questions posed by partner companies using their proprietary data, enabling students to gain valuable insights and become directly operational. This project boosts their career prospects. Masterclasses Masterclases will take place throughout the year at M2. Some examples are: Strategic Business Analytics, Data Security, Data Ethics Regulation, Data Driven Entrepreneurship, Business Ethics, AI in HR Management, Digital Economics Internships Master 1: 3 months Internship (Optional) This optional internship takes place at the end of Year 1 (M1) and allows you to put the knowledge and skills you have learned to practice in a real-life context. Master 2: 4 to 6 months Internship (or Professional Experience) Your internship can take place anywhere in the world and is designed to boost your professional integration. Through the developed network of ESSEC and of CentraleSupélecs partnering firms, institutions, and alumni, you are sure to easily find an internship that suits your career ambitions. International Study TripThe International Field Trip is a one-week trip in M2 to meet key actors, local professionals and business leaders all over the world, and confront your knowledge of best practices and emerging applications of analytics developing in other countries. Upon completion, students will be awarded two degrees: the Master in Data Sciences & Business Analytics from ESSEC I CentraleSupelec and the MS degree in Business Analytics from Columbia. After studying the first period at ESSEC | CentraleSupelec, students who wish to participate in the dual degree must submit an application in February and will go through a pre-selection process run by ESSEC I CentraleSupelec. The final selection will be made by Columbia University. Students will pay tuition and fees each academic year to the Institution where they are enrolled. This is the first association of its kind to bridge the two schools. The objective of DOT is to allow students from all backgrounds at ESSEC and CentraleSupélec to gain a thorough understanding of the domain of data and its different applications. As our world revolves increasingly around data collection, mining, predictions, and interpretations, it is essential for leaders of tomorrow to fully grasp data-oriented thinking. ESSEC Career Services Throughout your time at ESSEC, the Career Services will accompany you in defining your career plan and facilitating your entry into the professional world. Career guidance and advice ESSEC Career Services provides orientation and support to help students find suitable positions upon graduating. These services include personal development coaching which has been designed to help students capitalize on their skills and experience, so they become conscious of their assets. By defining a personal strategy to market their skills, students optimize their chances of succeeding on their chosen career path.The Career Services also organize individual counseling, workshops, mock interviews, conferences and opportunities to meet with executive search consultants, industry leaders/CEOs and HR Directors. Each year, there are: 25,000 exclusive job postings: internships, apprenticeships, graduate programs, V.I.E and jobs 450+ meetings with recruiters based in France and all around the world: job fairs, company presentations and case studies Nearly 4,000 individual appointments with career consultants An access to 3 learning platforms and 50+ articles, training and self-teaching modules.200+ career-related workshop ESSEC Alumni: A network For Life When you join ESSEC Business School, you join a community and will discover the power of the ESSEC network. ESSEC Alumni already has 71,000 graduates with diverse profiles dispersed in all corners of the world. With unique personalities, they share a common goal: to achieve their career objectives. As you enter ESSEC, you become a member of ESSEC Alumni and you remain one forever. This is the lifetime membership, that ESSEC has been the first French Business School with a global reach to put in place. ESSEC Alumni is by your side at every stage of your career: When you are a student, to guide you in finding professional opportunities through the network, exchanging with graduates, benefiting from various services to launch your start-up, and staying up to date with the latest news from the ESSEC community. When you are a graduate, to support you throughout your professional life, help you develop your network and exchange with your peers, guide you in benefiting from services for your start-up, and allow you to rediscover the atmosphere of your ESSEC years. STEP 1: Anticipate, prepare and take the testsYou will need to provide:- 1 Management test score - mandatory- 1 English test score - mandatory. The English test is not required if the applicant has spent at least 3 years in a higher education program completely taught in English. In that case, please provide us an official certificate with the mention that the medium of instruction is English. TEST VALIDITY* Management Test GMAT Exam, GMAT, GMAT Online, or GMAT Focus Edition 5 years Select "ESSEC Business School-Master in Data Sciences & Business Analytics" GRE or GRE Test at Home (Verbal Reasoning, Quantitative Reasoning and Analytical Writing) 5 years Institution Code: 0839 Tage-Mage 2 years English Test TOEFL iBT, TOEFL iBT Special at Home Edition The English tests must not be older than 2 years at the application deadline (application round you choose to apply in) Minimum score 95 Institution Code: 0520 IELTS Academic Minimum score 6.5 Cambridge B2 First Minimum Minimum score 175 TOEIC Listening and Reading Minimum score 850 *The tests must be valid at the time of closing of the application session. It can take several months to prepare and register for an exam slot for these tests. Keep this in mind before starting your application as without these test scores uploaded in your application file, it will be incomplete. Click here to take the GMAT Quiz and get an estimate of your score. Please note that you cannot apply with a GMAT Quiz score. STEP 2: Start your online applicationCreate your candidate account. You can fill in the online application at your own pace and come back to it at any point. You can only apply once per program each academic year. Once validated, your campus choice is final. Once submitted, your campus and track choices are final. STEP 3: Upload Your Supporting DocumentsA complete application file includes the following items. Incomplete application will not be processed. All documents must be provided in English or French (except the CV, which must be provided in English only). Official translations must be provided for documents in other languages by a certified translator. Items Description Curriculum Vitae 1 page maximum - in English Degree(s) obtained Authenticated copies of accredited degrees since high school (school leaving). While applying, if you do not have your final diploma that makes you eligible for the program, you can apply with an Enrolment Certificate, with an expected graduation date. Important: By mid-December of your starting year at ESSEC, you will have to provide a copy of your diploma (or a certificate of completion). Transcripts/Grade Sheets Upload Authenticated copies of official transcripts, in chronological order, for all academic terms attended since high school, including exchange programs, repeated years, preparatory classes, grading system details and double degree (simple copies and screenshots are not accepted). If your studies have been interrupted, please add a letter with the academic year concerned and explain the reasons (gap year, illness, change of direction, travel, employment, leave, internship, etc.). 2 x References One academic and one professional reference is highly recommended. It is the applicants responsibility to enter details of both the referees as soon as possible to allow them to send the online recommendation on time. Once you enter their details and save, a link is sent to them immediately to fill out the recommendation online. 1 Management Test Copy of official score (test taker version) 1 English Test 1 Certificate for Athletes (if applicable) A certificate for High Level Athlete (HLA) or Certificate of Aptitude for Sports Practice is required. The certificate must be valid at the time of application. 1 Identity Card Passport or National Identity Card (only for EU citizens) 1 Photograph A recent ID photo Application Fee €100 non-refundable and payable online onlyClick to see if you are exempted STEP 4: Submit your applicationOnce you have completed your online application and have attached all the supporting documents, the final step is to submit your online application. Once you have submitted your application online, you cannot make changes to your application. Please keep in mind that there are several rounds of admissions. The deadlines to submit your application are listed in the table above. STEP 5: Your application file is ready for reviewOnce submitted, your application will be reviewed by the admission committee. Each part of your application is taken into account, hence the need to complete it conscientiously. Kindly note that if a clarification is needed, an interview may be scheduled. STEP 6: Get your resultsYour application will be assessed by the Academic Directors and an admissions committee. You will be notified about the results by email (refer to the above mentioned calendar). If you have been successful, you will then be contacted by the Admissions Office to inform you how to confirm your place in the program. If you applied for one-year program, please note that if the commission board finds that your experience or background is strong but not complete enough in some required aspects, you may be asked to join the two-year program instead in order to build up your strength and ensure your success. Please note that once your admission is confirmed, you will not be able to change tracks anymore. Step 7: Secure your seatFollowing your admission, make sure to secure your seat in the program by paying the non-refundable deposit within 2 weeks. This amount will be deducted from your tuition fee. Do you need more information?You need more information to prepare your application? Please refer to this link for insights on our application portal. How important are the references?References are very important. The admissions committee is used to looking at these and the ones that make the difference outline concrete examples of how the student lives up to the praise/recommendations given. You should therefore select references who know you best and have experience of working with you either academically or professionally. It is much better to have a reference from someone who knows you than from someone you have selected due to their position. How important is the GMAT score?The GMAT is a very important part of your application. It is mandatory and we encourage you to get ready for the GMAT exam in advance. You should aim for as high a GMAT score as you can possibly achieve. Is a certain level of French required for the program?No, the program is taught in English and all of the staff members speak English. You have the chance to learn French during your program.However, we strongly recommend you try and learn French when you are here. Acquiring the language does help you during your time at ESSEC and in France. If you want to remain in France for your internship or job in the future, learning French is fundamental. How will my application be evaluated?Every application is thoroughly reviewed by the admissions board which is composed of both academic and professional staff, with consideration given to all elements including hard and soft skills. Eligibility: All female students with a citizenship of a country in Asia, Latin America, Africa and Europe (excluding France), who have obtained or are currently pursuing a non-French degree. EIFFEL ScholarshipDESCRIPTION: The French Ministry of Foreign Affairs funds EIFFEL scholarship. ELIGIBILITY: Reserved for non-French candidates, double nationality included, no older than 30 years old at the time the selection committee will meet (around mid-March). AMOUNT: A monthly allowance of €1,181 and covered costs of one international return journey and social security cover. PROCEDURE: ESSEC submits applications for EIFFEL scholarships on your behalf. Your application should be completed and submitted therefore in the first round of applications. Student Loans FranceAs an ESSEC student, you can take out a preferential rate bank loan, which covers full tuition and is repaid starting at the end of your first year of work. Loan applicants are required to have a guarantor living in France. According to the banks, the guarantor must earn enough to cover the monthly loan payments but also either be a French citizen, a close family member and/or both. Additional fees and expenses will be the responsibility of the student. Prodigy FinanceInternational Students from 150 different nationalities admitted to the Master in Finance may now apply to Prodigy Finance loans. Contrary to the banks in France, Prodigy does not require a collateral or co-signer. These loans are granted on the students future earning potential and do not take into account credit history. Students may apply online on the Prodigy website. There is no hidden fee or early repayment fee. Interest rates may vary depending on individual profiles. Funds are directly disbursed to the school in euro (€) so no exchange rates are borne by the student. Disbursement starts from September and loan application processing time may go up to a month and a half. The sooner you apply, the better. We advise you to carefully read the Prodigy website to check your eligibility before applying. US Federal & Private LoansMany US citizens or permanent residents opt to take out the US Federal Stafford and private Sallie Mae loans. These loans can cover up to the full cost of attendance and all applicants having a co-signer in the US are eligible for these loan programmes. ESSEC is listed as “ESSEC Business School", and has a code number of G30959. L’ampleur, la vitesse et la profondeur des transformations du monde sont inédites. Pour accompagner le changement et accélérer les transitions, des milliers d’acteurs se mobilisent et mettent leurs compétences au service de nouveaux modèles pour notre économie et notre société, alliant la conscience de l’urgence et le courage de bâtir un monde plus juste et durable. C’est pour répondre à ces besoins que l’ESSEC et CY- Cergy Paris Université ont décidé de combiner les forces d’une grande école de management avec celles d’une université publique pluridisciplinaire pour co-créer une nouvelle formation d’excellence dédiée aux transitions : le Bachelor ACT”. Vincenzo VinziDirecteur généralESSEC Business School Laurent GatineauPrésident de CYCergy Paris Université Le Bachelor Act est une nouvelle formation Bac +3, délivrant un grade de licence, lancée par l’ESSEC et CY Cergy Paris Université. Pluridisciplinaire et fondée sur une pédagogie active et une approche par compétences, son objectif est de permettre aux étudiants de maîtriser la conduite de projets au service des transitions écologiques, citoyennes et sociétales. Le programme est enregistré au RNCP – Fiche RNCP37249(niveau 6). Le Bachelor ACT est visé et possède le grade de Licence. Formation pluri- et transdisciplinaire, le programme intègre, tant en modules séparés que mixtes : Les sciences de l’environnement (écologie, biologie, physique, ect.) pour comprendre le système terre et les liens entre le climat, l’activité humaine et le vivant ; Les sciences sociales (sociologie, économie, politiques, psychologie, philosophie…) pour comprendre les transitions et agir à l’échelle des sociétés et des organisations ; Les sciences de gestion (stratégie, management, finance, comptabilité, marketing, science de la décision…) pour apprendre à agir dans un environnement professionnel ; Les sciences appliquées : outils informatiques, numériques et travail collaboratif. Le Bachelor ACT combine cours théoriques et expérimentations terrain permettant d’acquérir des compétences professionnelles clés. Comprendre les enjeux des transitions à lère de lanthropocène Comprendre les enjeux systémiques du système terre et des liens entre le climat, la biodiversité et les sociétés humaines Comprendre les grands enjeux de société contemporains : la lutte contre la pauvreté, l’éducation, la biodiversité, l’égalité des chances, Comprendre les rôles, spécificités, les enjeux et les relations des sociaux, environnementaux d’une activité humaine Concevoir et piloter un projet Maîtriser le processus et les outils du design thinking Piloter un projet (charte, objectifs, planification, analyse de risques, répartition des rôles) Construire collectivement une vision partagée et formuler une raison d’être Définir un modèle économique vertueux au service d’un projet social et/ou environnemental mettre en oeuvre une dynamique d’actions collectives originales et créatives sur un territoire (community organizing) Trouver sa voie et ce qui nous anime Apprendre à se connaître et à s’estimer Clarifier ses projets personnels et professionnels Développer une posture apprenante et résiliente Incarner avec indulgence le changement qu’on veut voir dans le monde Chaque étudiant apprend à mener des projets et à cultiver son esprit d’initiative, par des expériences concrètes, des modules de cours donnés par des enseignants et des professionnels engagés, des projets collectifs, des immersions, des rencontres, des engagements personnels. S’appuyant sur une pédagogie innovante, active et collaborative, le programme permet à chaque étudiant de construire ses projets d’avenir en accord avec sa personnalité, tout en trouvant sa voie dans le collectif. Cela passe par des formats d’apprentissage variés et complémentaires : projets collectifs en situation réelle, immersions et visites terrains, modules d’exploration libre, séminaires collectifs, agora, classes inversées, module en autogestion, accompagnement personnalisé… Le programme permet de personnaliser son parcours de formation. C’est un parcours exigeant et très riche. La possibilité de faire un échange universitaire à l’international ou une année en alternance (et donc de faire financer sa formation).Les missions professionnelles sont déterminantes dans le cursus des étudiants du Bachelor ACT. Au cours des 3 ans, ils devront effectuer plusieurs stages pour pouvoir mettre en pratique les enseignements au sein d’une structure. L’alternance est également proposée en 3ème année.Les stages : Durant les 3 ans de Bachelor, plusieurs stages doivent être effectués d’une durée de 3 à 4 mois au sein d’une entreprise, d’une association ou d’une collectivité. Au total, les étudiants réalisent entre 9 et 16 mois de stage tout au long de leur scolarité. A cela s’ajoutent des missions et des projets en situation réelle qui viennent enrichir les compétences et l’expérience professionnelle des étudiants. La 3ème année du Bachelor ACT : Lors de la 3ème année, les étudiants ont le choix entre réaliser : Leur cinquième semestre en échange universitaire. Leur cinquième semestre en stage dans une organisation à l’étranger. Leur 3ème année en alternance. Limmersion internationale est un élément clé de la pédagogie du programme. Elle vous prépare à aborder une carrière professionnelle à linternational dans les meilleures dispositions et vous permet dapprendre à évoluer au sein denvironnements multiculturels. Répartie tout au long du parcours, cette expérience à linternational peut être menée sous la forme de stages ou déchanges à létranger. Les échanges universitaires Au cours de sa scolarité, chaque étudiant pourra effectuer son semestre en échange universitaire au sein de lune des universités partenaires. Les expériences professionnelles à l’international Chaque année, les étudiants peuvent effectuer leur stage à létranger avec pour objectif de préparer une carrière à l’international. De manière plus exceptionnelle, l’apprentissage peut aussi être réalisé à l’étranger si l’entreprise a un statut juridique français.Les enseignements se dérouleront sur le campus de l’ESSEC et de CY Cergy Paris Université (site Bernard Hirsch). Les campus sont situés à 40 minutes en train (RER) du centre de Paris à Cergy, 2ᵉ pôle universitaire d’Ile-de-France qui accueille 27 000 étudiants. Au cœur de la ville, les 2 campus sont à quelques minutes à pieds l’un de l’autre. De son côté, le campus de l’ESSEC dispose de nombreux services : résidences étudiantes, infrastructures sportives (gymnase, courts de tennis, salle de sport), cafétéria, Learning Center (espace de créativité, de partage de la connaissance)… Les étudiants pourront bénéficier d’infrastructures modernes à la pointe de la technologie. Ce campus bénéficie également de son propre écosystème dédié à l’entrepreneuriat, à l’innovation sociale et écologique. ainsi qu’à l’égalité, la diversité et l’inclusion. Le campus Hirsch de CY accueille quant à lui l’Institut National du Professorat et de l’Education (INSPE). Les étudiants pourront bénéficier de la dynamique de ce campus ainsi que des infrastructures telles que la bibliothèque, le restaurant universitaire CROUS et les espaces verts aux alentours. CY Cergy Paris Université accompagne également les initiatives étudiantes, notamment à travers son réseau de FabLabs dont LabBoite qui se trouve à proximité des 2 campus. Vie associative Au fil des années, les promotions successives des 2 établissements ont fondé et gèrent plus d’une centaine de clubs et associations aux thématiques très variées : sportives, culturelles, humanitaires, internationales ou encore citoyennes, il y en a pour tous les goûts ! Les étudiants du Bachelor ACT pourront y contribuer activement selon leurs préférences. Ils pourront aussi rejoindre le BDE du Bachelor ACT afin de mener des projets en lien avec les valeurs portées par la formation. La poursuite en MasterRiche d’un écosystème diversifié et d’une pédagogie par l’action, le Bachelor ACT est un programme exigeant, dans lequel chaque étudiant peut acquérir des savoir-faire transversaux qui lui assurent de nombreux débouchés. La formation offre la possibilité pour les diplômés de poursuivre leurs études en Master avec toutes les clés en main pour élargir leur domaine d’expertise en lien avec les sujets de transitions : Management (Master Management de la Responsabilité Sociale de lEntreprise (RSE) ; Master Economie Sociale et Solidaire (ESS)) Innovation et entrepreneuriat (Master Management de l’innovation, Master Entrepreneuriat social) Environnement (Master Aménagement et développement durable des territoires) Ressources humaines (Master Ressources humaine et bien-être au travail, Master Conduite du changement) Sciences sociales et politiques (Master Sciences politiques, Master Développement culturel territorial) Relations internationales (Master Affaires internationales, Master Coopération internationale) Communication & Marketing (Master Marketing et communication responsable, Master Journalisme) Pour en savoir plus. Des métiers davenir utiles pour la sociétéLe Bachelor ACT prépare les étudiants à la conduite de projets dans les transitions écologiques, citoyennes et sociétales pour agir : En entreprise dans des fonctions de stratégie, d’innovation, d’engagement, de diversité et dinclusion, liée à la raison d’être; Dans les collectivités territoriales, les administrations de l’État, les institutions européennes, dans le monde politique; Dans les institutions internationales ou les ONG d’envergure mondiale : UNESCO, OCDE, ONU, Banque Mondiale, etc.; Dans des cabinets de conseil et d’audit, cabinets d’étude, instituts de recherche ou organismes de régulation; Dans lEconomie Sociale et Solidaire : associations, des coopératives, des mutuelles Dans une start-up à impact, en tant qu’entrepreneur social ou chef de projet à impact Découvrez sur cette page une classification par enjeux de métiers envisageables directement après le Bachelor ACT ou après une spécialisation en Master. ESSEC Alumni, c’est déjà 71 000 diplômés aux parcours et profils très variés, dispersés dans les quatre coins du monde. Des personnalités uniques avec un but commun : atteindre ses objectifs de carrière ! Dès votre entrée à l’école, vous devenez membre d’ESSEC Alumni et le restez toujours. Si vous vous projeter dans une carrière engagée, dans les métiers du développement durable, de la responsabilité sociale, de l’économie sociale et solidaire, des institutions et collectivités ou encore des ONG. Étape 1 : Démarrez votre candidature Pour démarrer votre candidature, vous devez dabord créer votre compte en ligne.Votre dossier de candidature en ligne peut être complété en plusieurs étapes. Vous pouvez donc y revenir à tout moment jusqu’à la date de clôture des inscriptions. Une fois votre candidature validée (submit), vous ne pourrez plus la modifier.N’oubliez pas votre mot de passe, il vous sera demandé à chaque connexion. Étape 2 : Constituez votre dossier Chaque candidat devra déposer un dossier de candidature qui comprendra les documents suivants :• Pièce d’identité • Relevé de notes des 3 dernières années ;• Curriculum vitae• Diplôme du bac ou certificat de scolarité • Le score d’un test de langue française pour les candidats non francophones (DELF B2 , TCF score de 450 minimum). Les candidats non francophones ayant suivi au moins deux années détudes secondaires dans un programme enseigné en français sont exemptés.• Une lettre de recommandation optionnelle Frais de dossier : 40€ (candidats non boursiers), 20€ (candidats boursiers) *, non remboursables, payables en ligne. *sur justificatif pour lannée en cours 2024-2025 Étape 3 : Mise en situation écriteLes dossiers seront étudiés par un jury pour déterminer l’admissibilité des candidats.Les candidats admissibles seront invités à effectuer un exercice écrit de mise en situation dans le temps imparti. Cette mise en situation confronte le candidat à une série d’événements sur des thématiques environnementales, sociales et citoyennes, qui sont celles que couvre le Bachelor ACT. Étape 4 : Entretien de motivation Les candidats admissibles devront par la suite passer un entretien de motivation en ligne Étape 5 : Résultats d’admissionLes résultats d’admission vous seront communiqués par mail. Vous pouvez également les consulter en vous connectant sur votre Candidature en ligne. Étape 6 : Confirmez votre inscription Une fois admis, vous serez notifié par email par nos services pour confirmer votre inscription.Vous recevrez également les modalités pour le paiement en ligne des arrhes non remboursables. Les frais de candidature sont de: 40,00 € (candidats non boursiers) 20,00 € (candidats boursiers) Le règlement du montant de vos droits d’inscription s’effectue sur Parcoursup. Les bourses Exonérations partielles de frais de scolarité pour les boursiers CROUS En fonction des revenus du foyer fiscal dont vous dépendez, vous pouvez prétendre à une bourse qui peut couvrir jusqu’à 100% de vos droits de scolarité. Pour connaître le montant exact dexonération, consultez la FAQ. Bourse du CROUS Vous pourrez également avoir accès aux bourses du CROUS, pouvant atteindre 550€ par mois. Les demandes doivent être faites entre janvier et avril de lannée précédente auprès du CROUS de votre académie. Bourse de mobilité internationale Des bourses daides à la mobilité internationale aidant à financer un échange universitaire ou un stage à létranger sont versées notamment par le programme Erasmus. Ces aides peuvent aller jusquà 300€ par mois. Pour obtenir des renseignements, nhésitez pas à nous contacter. Bourse Mission Handicap En toute confidentialité, les étudiants en situation de handicap qui souhaitent suivre un programme de formation à lESSEC peuvent, après étude de leur dossier de candidature, obtenir une bourse d’étude ou bourse de compensation du handicap. Celles-ci peuvent couvrir les frais de scolarité et/ou des frais de vie. Pour plus de renseignements : elisabeth.forget@essec.edu L’apprentissageLors de la 3e année, les étudiants du Bachelor ACT, peuvent suivre leur cursus en apprentissage. Les contrats sont signés pour 12 mois et proposent un rythme alterné sur la base de 5 mois pleins en entreprise, 4 mois pleins en cours et 3 mois pleins en entreprise. Les frais de scolarité sont pris en charge par lentreprise qui accueille l’apprenti (hors frais annuels de médecine préventive qui sélèvent à 50€). L’apprentissage est un contrat passé entre vous et une entreprise qui vous permet dalterner les phases d’études et de travail selon des rythmes variés. One must be able to navigate through volatile, uncertain, complex, and ambiguous (VUCA) contexts with strategic thinking, critical reasoning, creativity, problem-solving, collaboration, and strong communication skills. ESSEC Business School’s Master in Strategy and Management of International Business (SMIB) program is ranked 3rd worldwide in 2024 by QS among Masters in Management programs and 1st in Asia. The program offers customized tracks and specializations that equip participants with solid analytical, digital, strategic, innovation, and entrepreneurial skill sets that are highly sought after in a competitive job market. As a student of SMIB, you will have the opportunity to participate in hands-on assignments and company projects, benefit from an outstanding learning experience, and learn from a world-class faculty. You will also join a global community of 71,000 ESSEC alumni, including more than 3,000 former SMIB participants. 20% hold degrees in Engineering, Sciences and Health 80% hold degrees in Law, Political Sciences, Finance, Economics, Business, Languages, Literature 34 nationalities 46% women 23 average age Masters Grade The Master in Strategy and Management of International Business (SMIB) program is authorized by the French Ministry of Higher Education and Research to award a recognised BAC+5 degree, Master’s Grade, to its students. Upon completion of the program, students would have accumulated a total of 300 ECTS to obtain a Master’s degree. Triple Crown Accreditation The academic excellence of ESSEC’s programs is recognized through its international standards in management training, and it holds the prestigious ”Triple Crown of accreditations: EQUIS, AACSB, and AMBA. “Welcome to France”- Campus France ESSEC Business School has been recognized by Campus France and the Ministry of Higher Education and Research for the quality of its international students’ welcome. The school received the highest level that can be obtained from the "Bienvenue en France" certification, which is the third level. This certification recognizes the quality of ESSECs reception in all the criteria provided: The quality and accessibility of information The welcoming of new international students The academic offer Accommodations Campus life The quality of post-graduate follow-up Academic Excellence Choice of a specialized track in France, Asia, or abroad each with a specific career goal in mind. The chance to mix with a highly diverse class and teaching faculty. Professional Experience A professional business mindset in all aspects of the program. Integrated professional experiences. International Exposure Exchange and double degree opportunities with leading academic partners. An international business study trip. Please note that the duration of the Master in SMIB is 2 years (Master 1 + Master 2) or 1 year (Master 2 only), depending on your background and latest degree. MASTER 1 (M1) in FRANCE A year to grasp the prerequisites of core business management and decide your specialisation for next year. Academic Courses | Case Studies | Workshops | Languages Business & Industry Chair in ESSEC Africa (optional) and Professional Experience (4-6 months) MASTER 2 (M2) in FRANCE or SINGAPORE A year to specialise and gain in-depth knowledge and experience integratingcritical thinking about sustainability and responsible leadership. Academic Courses | Professional Workshops | Business Simulation | Case Studies | Soft Skills Validate refreshers, core courses, and research seminars and choose from the following: OPTION 1: DOUBLE DEGREE OPTION 2: EXCHANGE OPTION 3: SPECIALISATIONS - EGADE in Mexico- USC in United States - Queens in Canada- CUHK in Hong Kong- ESSEC Africa in Morocco Global Business Management(in France or Singapore) Global Leadership and Sustainability(in France or Singapore) Global Entrepreneurship & Innovation(in France only) Electives Learning Expedition Professional Experience (4-6 months) Year 1 - Master 1 (M1) - ESSEC Cergy Campus (France)You will build your core competencies of business and understand how international complexity impacts business conduct. Through this first year, you will also discover your professional interests, to help you decide on which specialized track to choose in Year 2 (M2). Some courses: Strategic Tools for Strategy Building, Introduction to Data, Business Conduct - An International Perspective, Sustainable Development and Managerial Challenges, Geopolitics The M1 will be conclude by a 4-6 months professional experience and an option to carry out a Chair specialisation (Business & Industry Chair at ESSEC Africa campus located in Rabat, Morocco). Business and Industry (B&I) in Africa Chair in Rabat, Morocco Key details: - The courses will be taught in English- If students choose this chair, their M1 year will be as follows: August-December: Courses in Cergy January-March: Chair B&I in Africa in Rabat April-August: Internship (worldwide) September: Start of Year 2 (M2) - Students will apply in September and selection confirmation will be done by October. - All students of SMIB (Year 1) are eligible to apply. Description: The African continent is changing fast and offers many opportunities in a rapid geopolitical shift. The abundance and the role of raw materials and commodities has resulted in the acceleration of industrialization and logistics, financing needs, and human capital opportunities. This, in turn, results in the diversification of economies and the transformation of products in the global value chain. Tanger Med, for example, is a port complex located in the city of Tangier, Morocco. Since its inauguration in 2007, it has become one of the busiest ports in the Mediterranean region, with an annual capacity of over 9 million containers. It has been instrumental in boosting Moroccos economy, attracting foreign investment, and creating job opportunities. The port has also played a crucial role in enhancing trade between Europe, Africa, and Asia, in particular, in the automobile and aeronautic manufactures. The success of Tanger Med has inspired other African countries to invest in similar projects, such as the construction of the Lamu Port in Kenya and the Bagamoyo Port in Tanzania, demonstrating the potential of Africa. Year 2 - Master 2 (M2) - ESSEC Cergy Campus (France) September to December Students will validate common core track shared with students of different Masters programs. They also have to validate the core track of the program. Alongside, to better prepare for the specialisations, they have to take some refresher courses. These refresher courses help students joining from diverse academic backgrounds to have the same understanding of the theories and principles discussed during the class. Lastly, to conclude this period, students will also participate in some research seminars. January onward While students are validating the first term, in the month of October, they will take a decision to add a specialisation or further the international flavour in the program. They will choose between the following options from January onward:- OPTION 1: Choose a Double Degree1. Darla Moore School of Business, University of South Carolina (USC) in Columbia, South CarolinaShould they choose, students will join this track to continue their focus on International Business and who want to get positions in Economic Institutions, Financial Departments of MNCs or Investment Funds.
